      <section class="section section__sports content" data-section="section-sports" id="section__sports">
       <h2 class="section-title">
        Sports
       </h2>
       <div class="module module__lead" data-module="lead">
        <article class="article article--lead" data-article-id="B6GEW6PZV5HR3MJIJDQ6W7QHLI" data-ga-content-type="article" data-ga-module="sports" data-ga-section="sports" data-ga-url="https://www.syracuse.com/orangebasketball/2021/03/the-best-shooting-guard-in-the-nation-is-on-syracuse-what-theyre-saying-about-orange-win-in-ncaa-tournament.html" data-image-thumb="https://www.syracuse.com/resizer/_IeIbeWnFum96VcZ2VNRS0zjuK4=/300x225/smart/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/advancelocal/6CQ4CM5DNVGWVBZD6DFXWZAIJY.jpg" data-module="sports" data-publishedon="1616245241" data-section="sports" data-section-name="sports" data-social-hed="‘The best shooting guard in the nation is on Syracuse:’ What they’re saying about Orange in NCAA tournament" data-source="https://www.syracuse.com/orangebasketball/2021/03/the-best-shooting-guard-in-the-nation-is-on-syracuse-what-theyre-saying-about-orange-win-in-ncaa-tournament.html" data-type="article" id="article-B6GEW6PZV5HR3MJIJDQ6W7QHLI">
         <div class="article__picture article-picture--container">
         </div>
         <div class="article__label-wrap">
          <span class="article__label">
           Orange Basketball
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="article__details--headline">
          <h1>
           <a data-ga-content-type="article" data-linktype="headline" href="https://www.syracuse.com/orangebasketball/2021/03/the-best-shooting-guard-in-the-nation-is-on-syracuse-what-theyre-saying-about-orange-win-in-ncaa-tournament.html">
            ‘The best shooting guard in the nation is on Syracuse:’ What they’re saying about Orange in NCAA tournament
           </a>
          </h1>
         </div>
         <div class="article__details">
          <div class="article__details--summary">
           Buddy Boeheim and the zone defense were two main topics during after Syracuse's win over San Diego Stae in the first round.
          </div>
          <div class="article__details--byline">
           <span>
            <span>
             Syracuse.com
